        )\n                os.environ[self.name] = fallback\n        return super().get()\n\n\nclass EnvBoolWithAlias(_DeprecatedEnvFallback, EnvBool):\n    pass\n\n\nclass Under high concurrency (128 requests), the sender process can garbage-collect/free the backing tensor before the receiver (TP1 scheduler) has a chance to open the IPC handle, resulting in a stale device pointer → `HIP error: invalid device pointer`.\n\nWith `SGLANG_USE_IPC_POOL_HANDLE_CACHE=1`, the pool's persistent IPC handle (backed by `MmItemMemoryPool.memory_pool`, allocated once at startup and never freed) is passed through to the proxy.
